(**********************************************************************************

 The two-sided displayed category of lenses

 Reference for lenses:
   https://ncatlab.org/nlab/show/lens+%28in+computer+science%29

 We define the two-sided displayed category of lenses.

 Contents
 1. Definition via two-sided displayed categories
 2. Discreteness and univalence
 3. Builders and accessors
 4. Identity and composition of lenses
 5. Identity and composition laws of lenses

 **********************************************************************************)

C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
(λ D : C → C → UU,
 ∏ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ : C,
 D x₁ y₁ → D x₂ y₂ → C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧ → C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧ → UU)
  (λ s v : C, C ⟦ s, v ⟧)
 exact (λ s₁ s₂ v₁ v₂ g₁ g₂ f₁ f₂, g₁ · f₂ = f₁ · g₂).
  Defined.

s₁, s₂, s₃, v₁, v₂, v₃: C
g₁: C ⟦ s₁, v₁ ⟧

g₃: C ⟦ s₃, v₃ ⟧
f₁: C ⟦ s₁, s₂ ⟧
f₂: C ⟦ s₂, s₃ ⟧
h₁: C ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
h₂: C ⟦ v₂, v₃ ⟧
p₁: g₁ · h₁ = f₁ · g₂
p₂: g₂ · h₂ = f₂ · g₃
g₁ · (h₁ · h₂) = f₁ · f₂ · g₃

C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
(λ D : C → C → UU,
 ∏ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ : C,
 D x₁ y₁ → D x₂ y₂ → C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧ → C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧ → UU)
  (λ s v : C, C ⟦ prodC v s, s ⟧)
 exact (λ s₁ s₂ v₁ v₂ g₁ g₂ f₁ f₂,
             g₁ · f₁
             =
             BinProductOfArrows _ _ _ f₂ f₁ · g₂).
  Defined.

s, v: C
g: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses_put_ob_mor s v
g · identity s =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v s) (prodC v s)
  (identity v) (identity s) · g

s, v: C
g: twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses_put_ob_mor s v
identity (prodC v s) =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v s) (prodC v s)
  (identity v) (identity s)

        use BinProductArrowUnique ; rewrite id_left, id_right ; apply idpath.

prodC: BinProducts C
twosided_disp_cat_comp
  twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses_put_ob_mor
 
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s₁, s₂, s₃, v₁, v₂, v₃: C
g₁: C ⟦ prodC v₁ s₁, s₁ ⟧
g₂: C ⟦ prodC v₂ s₂, s₂ ⟧
g₃: C ⟦ prodC v₃ s₃, s₃ ⟧
f₁: C ⟦ s₁, s₂ ⟧
f₂: C ⟦ s₂, s₃ ⟧
h₁: C ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
h₂: C ⟦ v₂, v₃ ⟧
p₁: g₁ · f₁ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₂ s₂) 
  (prodC v₁ s₁) h₁ f₁ · g₂
p₂: g₂ · f₂ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) 
  (prodC v₂ s₂) h₂ f₂ · g₃
g₁ · (f₁ · f₂) =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) (prodC v₁ s₁)
  (h₁ · h₂) (f₁ · f₂) · g₃

      
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s₁, s₂, s₃, v₁, v₂, v₃: C
g₁: C ⟦ prodC v₁ s₁, s₁ ⟧
g₂: C ⟦ prodC v₂ s₂, s₂ ⟧
g₃: C ⟦ prodC v₃ s₃, s₃ ⟧
f₁: C ⟦ s₁, s₂ ⟧
f₂: C ⟦ s₂, s₃ ⟧
h₁: C ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
h₂: C ⟦ v₂, v₃ ⟧
p₁: g₁ · f₁ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₂ s₂) 
  (prodC v₁ s₁) h₁ f₁ · g₂
p₂: g₂ · f₂ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) 
  (prodC v₂ s₂) h₂ f₂ · g₃
g₁ · f₁ · f₂ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) (prodC v₁ s₁)
  (h₁ · h₂) (f₁ · f₂) · g₃

      
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s₁, s₂, s₃, v₁, v₂, v₃: C
g₁: C ⟦ prodC v₁ s₁, s₁ ⟧
g₂: C ⟦ prodC v₂ s₂, s₂ ⟧
g₃: C ⟦ prodC v₃ s₃, s₃ ⟧
f₁: C ⟦ s₁, s₂ ⟧
f₂: C ⟦ s₂, s₃ ⟧
h₁: C ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
h₂: C ⟦ v₂, v₃ ⟧
p₁: g₁ · f₁ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₂ s₂) 
  (prodC v₁ s₁) h₁ f₁ · g₂
p₂: g₂ · f₂ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) 
  (prodC v₂ s₂) h₂ f₂ · g₃
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₂ s₂) (prodC v₁ s₁) h₁ f₁
· g₂ · f₂ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) (prodC v₁ s₁)
  (h₁ · h₂) (f₁ · f₂) · g₃

      
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s₁, s₂, s₃, v₁, v₂, v₃: C
g₁: C ⟦ prodC v₁ s₁, s₁ ⟧
g₂: C ⟦ prodC v₂ s₂, s₂ ⟧
g₃: C ⟦ prodC v₃ s₃, s₃ ⟧
f₁: C ⟦ s₁, s₂ ⟧
f₂: C ⟦ s₂, s₃ ⟧
h₁: C ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
h₂: C ⟦ v₂, v₃ ⟧
p₁: g₁ · f₁ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₂ s₂) 
  (prodC v₁ s₁) h₁ f₁ · g₂
p₂: g₂ · f₂ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) 
  (prodC v₂ s₂) h₂ f₂ · g₃
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₂ s₂) (prodC v₁ s₁) h₁ f₁
· (g₂ · f₂) =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) (prodC v₁ s₁)
  (h₁ · h₂) (f₁ · f₂) · g₃

      
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s₁, s₂, s₃, v₁, v₂, v₃: C
g₁: C ⟦ prodC v₁ s₁, s₁ ⟧
g₂: C ⟦ prodC v₂ s₂, s₂ ⟧
g₃: C ⟦ prodC v₃ s₃, s₃ ⟧
f₁: C ⟦ s₁, s₂ ⟧
f₂: C ⟦ s₂, s₃ ⟧
h₁: C ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
h₂: C ⟦ v₂, v₃ ⟧
p₁: g₁ · f₁ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₂ s₂) 
  (prodC v₁ s₁) h₁ f₁ · g₂
p₂: g₂ · f₂ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) 
  (prodC v₂ s₂) h₂ f₂ · g₃
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₂ s₂) (prodC v₁ s₁) h₁ f₁
· (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) (prodC v₂ s₂) h₂
     f₂ · g₃) =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) (prodC v₁ s₁)
  (h₁ · h₂) (f₁ · f₂) · g₃

      
C: category

s₁, s₂, s₃, v₁, v₂, v₃: C

p₂: g₂ · f₂ =

· BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) (prodC v₂ s₂) h₂
    f₂ · g₃ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) (prodC v₁ s₁)
  (h₁ · h₂) (f₁ · f₂) · g₃

h₁: C ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧

BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₂ s₂) 
  (prodC v₁ s₁) h₁ f₁ · g₂
p₂: g₂ · f₂ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) 
  (prodC v₂ s₂) h₂ f₂ · g₃
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) (prodC v₁ s₁)
  (h₁ · h₂) (f₁ · f₂) · g₃ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₃ s₃) (prodC v₁ s₁)
  (h₁ · h₂) (f₁ · f₂) · g₃

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

  Definition twosided_disp_cat_of_lawless_lenses
    : twosided_disp_cat C C
    := prod_of_twosided_disp_cat
         twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses_get
         twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses_put.

  Definition lenses_laws
             {s v : C}
             (l : twosided_disp_cat_of_lawless_lenses s v)
    : UU
    := let g := pr1 l in
       let p := pr2 l in
       (p · g = BinProductPr1 _ _)
       ×
       (BinProductArrow _ _ g (identity s) · p = identity s)
       ×
       (BinProductOfArrows
          _
          (prodC v _)
          (prodC _ _)
          (identity v)
          p
        · p
        =
        BinProductArrow
          _ _
          (BinProductPr1 _ _)
          (BinProductPr2 _ _ · BinProductPr2 _ _)
        · p).

  
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
l: twosided_disp_cat_of_lawless_lenses s v
isaprop (lenses_laws l)

  
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
l: twosided_disp_cat_of_lawless_lenses s v
isaprop (lenses_laws l)

    repeat (apply isapropdirprod) ; apply homset_property.
  Qed.

  twosided_disp_cat_of_lawless_lenses → UU

    exact (λ x, lenses_laws (pr22 x)).
  Defined.

  Definition twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses
    : twosided_disp_cat C C
    := sigma_twosided_disp_cat
         twosided_disp_cat_of_lawless_lenses
         disp_cat_of_lenses_laws.

C: category

      exact (!fg).
    
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
xy₁: C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
f: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
Hf: is_z_isomorphism f
Hg: is_z_isomorphism g
fg: xy₁ · g = f · xy₂
fg ;;2 (! z_iso_inv_on_right x₁ x₂ y₁ (f,, Hf)
            (xy₂ · inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg)) xy₁
            (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧)
               ((f,, Hf)
                · (xy₂ · inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg)))
               ((f,, Hf) · xy₂
                · inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
               (λ p : C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧, xy₁ = p)
               (z_iso_inv_on_left x₁ y₁ y₂ xy₁
                  (g,, Hg) ((f,, Hf) · xy₂)
                  (! fg
                   :
                   (f,, Hf) · xy₂ = xy₁ · (g,, Hg)))
               (assoc (f,, Hf) xy₂
                  (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))))) =
trb₂ id_two_disp xy₁
 apply homset_property.
    
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
xy₁: C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
xy₂: C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
f: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
Hf: is_z_isomorphism f
Hg: is_z_isomorphism g
fg: xy₁ · g = f · xy₂
! z_iso_inv_on_right x₁ x₂ y₁ (f,, Hf)
    (xy₂ · inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg)) xy₁
    (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧)
       ((f,, Hf) · (xy₂ · inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg)))
       ((f,, Hf) · xy₂ · inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
       (λ p : C ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧, xy₁ = p)
       (z_iso_inv_on_left x₁ y₁ y₂ xy₁ (g,, Hg)
          ((f,, Hf) · xy₂)
          (! fg : (f,, Hf) · xy₂ = xy₁ · (g,, Hg)))
       (assoc (f,, Hf) xy₂ (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg)))) ;;2 fg =
trb₂ id_two_disp xy₂
 apply homset_property.
  Qed.

                                       (prodC y₂ x₂)
                                     · identity y₂)
                                    (BinProductPr2 C
                                       (prodC y₂ x₂)
                                     · identity x₂)
                                    (identity
                                       (prodC y₂ x₂))
                                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                                       (C
                                        ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂,
                                        y₂ ⟧)
                                       (identity (...)
                                        · BinProductPr1
                                            C (...))
                                       (BinProductPr1
                                          C
                                          (prodC y₂ x₂))
                                       (λ p : C ⟦ ...,
                                              y₂ ⟧,
                                        p = ... · ...)
                                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                                          (C ⟦ ..., y₂
                                           ⟧)
                                          (... · ...)
                                          (BinProductPr1
                                             C ...)
                                          (λ ..., ...)
                                          (idpath ...)
                                          (id_right
                                             ...))
                                       (id_left
                                          (BinProductPr1
                                             C ...)))
                                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                                       (C
                                        ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂,
                                        x₂ ⟧)
                                       (identity (...)
                                        · BinProductPr2
                                            C (...))
                                       (BinProductPr2
                                          C
                                          (prodC y₂ x₂))
                                       (λ p : C ⟦ ...,
                                              x₂ ⟧,
                                        p = ... · ...)
                                       (internal_paths_rew_r
                                          (C ⟦ ..., x₂
                                           ⟧)
                                          (... · ...)
                                          (BinProductPr2
                                             C ...)
                                          (λ ..., ...)
                                          (idpath ...)
                                          (id_right
                                             ...))
                                       (id_left
                                          (BinProductPr2
                                             C ...))))
                                 (z_iso_after_z_iso_inv
                                    (f,, Hf)))
                              (z_iso_after_z_iso_inv
                                 (g,, Hg)))
                           (BinProductOfArrows_comp C
                              prodC y₂ x₂ y₁ x₁ y₂ x₂
                              (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
                              (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf))
                              g f)) xy₂)
                     (assoc
                        (BinProductOfArrows C
                           (prodC y₁ x₁) (prodC y₂ x₂)
                           (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
                           (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf)))
                        (BinProductOfArrows C
                           (prodC y₂ x₂) (prodC y₁ x₁)
                           g f) xy₂)) fg)
               (assoc'
                  (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁)
                     (prodC y₂ x₂)
                     (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
                     (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf))) xy₁ f)
             :
             xy₂ =
             BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁)
               (prodC y₂ x₂) (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
               (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf)) · xy₁
             · (f,, Hf))) = trb₂ id_two_disp xy₁
 apply homset_property.
    
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
xy₁: C ⟦ prodC y₁ x₁, x₁ ⟧
xy₂: C ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧
f: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
g: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
Hf: is_z_isomorphism f
Hg: is_z_isomorphism g
fg: xy₁ · f =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₂ x₂) 
  (prodC y₁ x₁) g f · xy₂
! z_iso_inv_on_left (prodC y₂ x₂) x₁ x₂
    (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁) (prodC y₂ x₂)
       (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
       (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf)) · xy₁) (f,, Hf) xy₂
    (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
       (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁)
          (prodC y₂ x₂) (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
          (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf)) · xy₁ · f)
       (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁)
          (prodC y₂ x₂) (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
          (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf)) · (xy₁ · f))
       (λ p : C ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧, xy₂ = p)
       (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ prodC y₁ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
          (xy₁ · f)
          (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₂ x₂)
             (prodC y₁ x₁) g f · xy₂)
          (λ p : C ⟦ prodC y₁ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
           xy₂ =
           BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁)
             (prodC y₂ x₂) (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
             (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf)) · p)
          (internal_paths_rew_r
             (C ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
             (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁)
                (prodC y₂ x₂)
                (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
                (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf))
              · (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₂ x₂)
                   (prodC y₁ x₁) g f · xy₂))
             (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁)
                (prodC y₂ x₂)
                (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
                (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf))
              · BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₂ x₂)
                  (prodC y₁ x₁) g f · xy₂)
             (λ p : C ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧, xy₂ = p)
             (! id_left xy₂ @
              maponpaths_2 compose
                (internal_paths_rew_r
                   (C ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂, prodC y₂ x₂ ⟧)
                   (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁)
                      (prodC y₂ x₂)
                      (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
                      (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf))
                    · BinProductOfArrows C
                        (prodC y₂ x₂) (prodC y₁ x₁) g
                        f)
                   (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₂ x₂)
                      (prodC y₂ x₂)
                      (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg) · g)
                      (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf) · f))
                   (λ p : C ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂, prodC y₂ x₂
                          ⟧,
                    identity (prodC y₂ x₂) = p)
                   (internal_paths_rew_r
                      (C ⟦ y₂, y₂ ⟧)
                      (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg)
                       · (g,, Hg)) (identity y₂)
                      (λ p : C ⟦ y₂, y₂ ⟧,
                       identity (prodC y₂ x₂) =
                       BinProductOfArrows C
                         (prodC y₂ x₂) (prodC y₂ x₂) p
                         (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf) · f))
                      (internal_paths_rew_r
                         (C ⟦ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
                         (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf)
                          · (f,, Hf)) (identity x₂)
                         (λ p : C ⟦ x₂, x₂ ⟧,
                          identity (prodC y₂ x₂) =
                          BinProductOfArrows C
                            (prodC y₂ x₂)
                            (prodC y₂ x₂)
                            (identity y₂) p)
                         (BinProductArrowUnique C y₂
                            x₂ (prodC y₂ x₂)
                            (prodC y₂ x₂)
                            (BinProductPr1 C
                               (prodC y₂ x₂)
                             · identity y₂)
                            (BinProductPr2 C
                               (prodC y₂ x₂)
                             · identity x₂)
                            (identity (prodC y₂ x₂))
                            (internal_paths_rew_r
                               (C ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
                               (identity (prodC y₂ x₂)
                                · BinProductPr1 C
                                    (prodC y₂ x₂))
                               (BinProductPr1 C
                                  (prodC y₂ x₂))
                               (λ p : C ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂,
                                      y₂ ⟧,
                                p =
                                BinProductPr1 C ...
                                · identity y₂)
                               (internal_paths_rew_r
                                  (C ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂, y₂
                                   ⟧)
                                  (BinProductPr1 C ...
                                   · identity y₂)
                                  (BinProductPr1 C
                                     (...))
                                  (λ p : ..., ... = p)
                                  (idpath (...))
                                  (id_right (...)))
                               (id_left
                                  (BinProductPr1 C
                                     (...))))
                            (internal_paths_rew_r
                               (C ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂, x₂ ⟧)
                               (identity (prodC y₂ x₂)
                                · BinProductPr2 C
                                    (prodC y₂ x₂))
                               (BinProductPr2 C
                                  (prodC y₂ x₂))
                               (λ p : C ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂,
                                      x₂ ⟧,
                                p =
                                BinProductPr2 C ...
                                · identity x₂)
                               (internal_paths_rew_r
                                  (C ⟦ prodC y₂ x₂, x₂
                                   ⟧)
                                  (BinProductPr2 C ...
                                   · identity x₂)
                                  (BinProductPr2 C
                                     (...))
                                  (λ p : ..., ... = p)
                                  (idpath (...))
                                  (id_right (...)))
                               (id_left
                                  (BinProductPr2 C
                                     (...)))))
                         (z_iso_after_z_iso_inv
                            (f,, Hf)))
                      (z_iso_after_z_iso_inv (g,, Hg)))
                   (BinProductOfArrows_comp C prodC y₂
                      x₂ y₁ x₁ y₂ x₂
                      (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
                      (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf)) g f))
                xy₂)
             (assoc
                (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁)
                   (prodC y₂ x₂)
                   (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
                   (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf)))
                (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₂ x₂)
                   (prodC y₁ x₁) g f) xy₂)) fg)
       (assoc'
          (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁)
             (prodC y₂ x₂) (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
             (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf))) xy₁ f)
     :
     xy₂ =
     BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁) (prodC y₂ x₂)
       (inv_from_z_iso (g,, Hg))
       (inv_from_z_iso (f,, Hf)) · xy₁ · (f,, Hf)) ;;2 fg =
trb₂ id_two_disp xy₂
 apply homset_property.
  Qed.

  (** * 3. Builders and accessors *)
  Definition lens
             (s v : C)
    : UU
    := twosided_disp_cat_of_lenses s v.

  Definition lens_data
             (s v : C)
    : UU
    := s --> v × prodC v s --> s.

  Definition make_lens_data
             {s v : C}
             (get : s --> v)
             (put : prodC v s --> s)
    : lens_data s v
    := get ,, put.

  Coercion lens_to_data
           {s v : C}
           (l : lens s v)
    : lens_data s v
    := pr1 l.

  Definition lens_get
             {s v : C}
             (l : lens_data s v)
    : s --> v
    := pr1 l.

  Definition lens_put
             {s v : C}
             (l : lens_data s v)
    : prodC v s --> s
    := pr2 l.

  
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
l: lens s v
lens_put l · lens_get l = BinProductPr1 C (prodC v s)

  
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
l: lens s v
lens_put l · lens_get l = BinProductPr1 C (prodC v s)

    exact (pr12 l).
  Qed.

  
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
l: lens s v
BinProductArrow C (prodC v s) (lens_get l)
  (identity s) · lens_put l = identity s

  
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
l: lens s v
BinProductArrow C (prodC v s) (lens_get l)
  (identity s) · lens_put l = identity s

    exact (pr122 l).
  Qed.

  
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
l: lens s v
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v s) (prodC v (prodC v s))
  (identity v) (lens_put l) · lens_put l =
BinProductArrow C (prodC v s)
  (BinProductPr1 C (prodC v (prodC v s)))
  (BinProductPr2 C (prodC v (prodC v s))
   · BinProductPr2 C (prodC v s)) · lens_put l

  
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
l: lens s v
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v s) (prodC v (prodC v s))
  (identity v) (lens_put l) · lens_put l =
BinProductArrow C (prodC v s)
  (BinProductPr1 C (prodC v (prodC v s)))
  (BinProductPr2 C (prodC v (prodC v s))
   · BinProductPr2 C (prodC v s)) · lens_put l

    exact (pr222 l).
  Qed.

  Definition lens_mor
             {s₁ s₂ v₁ v₂ : C}
             (l₁ : lens s₁ v₁)
             (l₂ : lens s₂ v₂)
             (f : s₁ --> s₂)
             (g : v₁ --> v₂)
    : UU
    := l₁ -->[ f ][ g ] l₂.

  Definition make_lens_mor
             {s₁ s₂ v₁ v₂ : C}
             {l₁ : lens s₁ v₁}
             {l₂ : lens s₂ v₂}
             {f : s₁ --> s₂}
             {g : v₁ --> v₂}
             (p_get : lens_get l₁ · g = f · lens_get l₂)
             (p_put : lens_put l₁ · f
                      =
                      BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₂ s₂) (prodC v₁ s₁) g f · lens_put l₂)
    : lens_mor l₁ l₂ f g
    := (p_get ,, p_put) ,, tt.

  
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s₁, s₂, v₁, v₂: C
l₁: lens s₁ v₁
l₂: lens s₂ v₂
f: C ⟦ s₁, s₂ ⟧
g: C ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
fg: lens_mor l₁ l₂ f g
lens_get l₁ · g = f · lens_get l₂

  
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s₁, s₂, v₁, v₂: C
l₁: lens s₁ v₁
l₂: lens s₂ v₂
f: C ⟦ s₁, s₂ ⟧
g: C ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
fg: lens_mor l₁ l₂ f g
lens_get l₁ · g = f · lens_get l₂

    exact (pr11 fg).
  Qed.

  
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s₁, s₂, v₁, v₂: C
l₁: lens s₁ v₁
l₂: lens s₂ v₂
f: C ⟦ s₁, s₂ ⟧
g: C ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧

lens_put l₁ · f =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v₂ s₂) (prodC v₁ s₁) g f
· lens_put l₂

  
C: category

· lens_put l₂

    exact (pr21 fg).
  Qed.

     (identity (prodC z x))
     (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x))
   · BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y x)
       (prodC (prodC z x) x)
       (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z y) (prodC z x)
          (identity z) (lens_get l₁) · lens_put l₂)
       (identity x) · lens_put l₁)
· (BinProductArrow C (prodC (prodC z x) x)
     (identity (prodC z x))
     (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x))
   · BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y x)
       (prodC (prodC z x) x)
       (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z y) (prodC z x)
          (identity z) (lens_get l₁) · lens_put l₂)
       (identity x) · lens_put l₁) =
BinProductArrow C (prodC z x)
  (BinProductPr1 C (prodC z (prodC z x)))
  (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z (prodC z x))
   · BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x))
· (BinProductArrow C (prodC (prodC z x) x)
     (identity (prodC z x))
     (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x))
   · BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y x)
       (prodC (prodC z x) x)
       (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z y) (prodC z x)
          (identity z) (lens_get l₁) · lens_put l₂)
       (identity x) · lens_put l₁)

p₁:= lens_put_get l₁: lens_put l₁ · lens_get l₁ =
BinProductPr1 C (prodC y x)
p₂:= lens_put_put l₂: BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z y)
  (prodC z (prodC z y)) 
  (identity z) (lens_put l₂) · 
lens_put l₂ =

   · BinProductPr2 C (prodC z y)) · 
lens_put l₂

  (prodC y (prodC y x)) 
  (identity y) (lens_put l₁) ·

  (BinProductPr2 C (prodC y (prodC y x))
   · BinProductPr2 C (prodC y x)) · 
lens_put l₁
BinProductArrow C (prodC z y)
  (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z (prodC z y))
     (prodC z (prodC z x)) (identity z)
     (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z y) (prodC z x)
        (identity z) (lens_get l₁))
   · BinProductPr1 C (prodC z (prodC z y)))
  (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z (prodC z y))
     (prodC z (prodC z x)) (identity z)
     (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z y) (prodC z x)
        (identity z) (lens_get l₁))
   · (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z (prodC z y))
      · BinProductPr2 C (prodC z y))) · lens_put l₂ =

  (BinProductArrow C (prodC z y)
     (BinProductPr1 C (prodC z (prodC z x)))
     (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z (prodC z x))
      · BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x) · lens_get l₁)
   · lens_put l₂)
  (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z (prodC z x))
   · BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x)) =
BinProductArrow C (prodC y x)
  (BinProductArrow C (prodC z x)
     (BinProductPr1 C (prodC z (prodC z x)))
     (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z (prodC z x))
      · BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x))
   · identity (prodC z x)
   · (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z y) (prodC z x)
        (identity z) (lens_get l₁) · lens_put l₂))
  (BinProductArrow C (prodC z x)
     (BinProductPr1 C (prodC z (prodC z x)))
     (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z (prodC z x))
      · BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x))
   · BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x) · identity x)

l₂: lens y z

  (prodC y (prodC y x)) 
  (identity y) (lens_put l₁) ·

  (BinProductPr2 C (prodC y (prodC y x))
   · BinProductPr2 C (prodC y x)) · 
lens_put l₁

  (BinProductArrow C (prodC z y)
     (BinProductPr1 C (prodC z (prodC z x)))
     (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z (prodC z x))
      · BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x) · lens_get l₁)
   · lens_put l₂)
  (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z (prodC z x))
   · BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x)) =

  (BinProductArrow C (prodC z x)

      · BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x))
   · (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z y) (prodC z x)
        (identity z) (lens_get l₁) · lens_put l₂))
  (BinProductArrow C (prodC z x)

     (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z (prodC z x))
      · BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x))
   · BinProductPr2 C (prodC z x))

C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: C
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
v₃: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
l₁: lens x₁ y₁
l₂: lens y₁ z₁
l₃: lens x₂ y₂
l₄: lens y₂ z₂
φ: lens_mor l₁ l₃ v₁ v₂
ψ: lens_mor l₂ l₄ v₂ v₃
BinProductArrow C (prodC (prodC z₁ x₁) x₁)
  (identity (prodC z₁ x₁))
  (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z₁ x₁))
· BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁)
    (prodC (prodC z₁ x₁) x₁)
    (BinProductOfArrows C 
       (prodC z₁ y₁) (prodC z₁ x₁) 
       (identity z₁) (lens_get l₁) · 
     lens_put l₂) (identity x₁) · 
lens_put l₁ · v₁ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z₂ x₂) (prodC z₁ x₁) v₃ v₁
· (BinProductArrow C (prodC (prodC z₂ x₂) x₂)
     (identity (prodC z₂ x₂))
     (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z₂ x₂))
   · BinProductOfArrows C 
       (prodC y₂ x₂) (prodC (prodC z₂ x₂) x₂)
       (BinProductOfArrows C 
          (prodC z₂ y₂) 
          (prodC z₂ x₂) 
          (identity z₂) 
          (lens_get l₃) · 
        lens_put l₄) (identity x₂) · 
   lens_put l₃)

    (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z₂ x₂))
· BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₂ x₂)
    (prodC (prodC z₂ x₂) x₂)
    (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z₂ y₂) (prodC z₂ x₂)
       (identity z₂) (lens_get l₃) · lens_put l₄)
    (identity x₂) · lens_put l₃

      
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: C
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
v₃: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
l₁: lens x₁ y₁
l₂: lens y₁ z₁
l₃: lens x₂ y₂
l₄: lens y₂ z₂
φ: lens_mor l₁ l₃ v₁ v₂
ψ: lens_mor l₂ l₄ v₂ v₃
BinProductArrow C (prodC (prodC z₁ x₁) x₁)
  (identity (prodC z₁ x₁))
  (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z₁ x₁))
· BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₁ x₁)
    (prodC (prodC z₁ x₁) x₁)
    (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z₁ y₁) (prodC z₁ x₁)
       (identity z₁) (lens_get l₁) · lens_put l₂)
    (identity x₁)
· BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₂ x₂) (prodC y₁ x₁) v₂
    v₁ =
BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z₂ x₂) (prodC z₁ x₁) v₃ v₁
· BinProductArrow C (prodC (prodC z₂ x₂) x₂)
    (identity (prodC z₂ x₂))
    (BinProductPr2 C (prodC z₂ x₂))
· BinProductOfArrows C (prodC y₂ x₂)
    (prodC (prodC z₂ x₂) x₂)
    (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z₂ y₂) (prodC z₂ x₂)
       (identity z₂) (lens_get l₃) · lens_put l₄)
    (identity x₂)

      
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: C

v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧

    (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC z₂ y₂) (prodC z₂ x₂)
       (identity z₂) (lens_get l₃) · lens_put l₄)
    (identity x₂)

      
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: C

C: category

  (identity z₁ · v₃) (lens_get l₁ · v₂) =

  (v₃ · identity z₂) (v₁ · lens_get l₃)

  (lens_get l₁ · v₂) =

  (v₁ · lens_get l₃)

      
C: category

C: category
prodC: BinProducts C

ψ: lens_mor l₂ l₄ v₂ v₃
v₁ · lens_get l₃ = v₁ · lens_get l₃

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

  (** * 5. Identity and composition laws of lenses *)
  
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
f: lens s v
comp_lens (identity_lens s) f = f

  
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
f: lens s v
comp_lens (identity_lens s) f = f

    
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
f: lens s v
identity s · lens_get f = lens_get f
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
f: lens s v
BinProductArrow C (prodC (prodC v s) s)
  (identity (prodC v s)) 
  (BinProductPr2 C (prodC v s))
· BinProductOfArrows C (prodC s s)
    (prodC (prodC v s) s)
    (BinProductOfArrows C 
       (prodC v s) (prodC v s) 
       (identity v) (identity s) · 
     lens_put f) (identity s)
· BinProductPr1 C (prodC s s) = 
lens_put f

    
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
f: lens s v
identity s · lens_get f = lens_get f
 apply id_left.
    
C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
f: lens s v
BinProductArrow C (prodC (prodC v s) s)
  (identity (prodC v s)) (BinProductPr2 C (prodC v s))
· BinProductOfArrows C (prodC s s)
    (prodC (prodC v s) s)
    (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v s) (prodC v s)
       (identity v) (identity s) · lens_put f)
    (identity s) · BinProductPr1 C (prodC s s) =
lens_put f
 
C: category

     (prodC (prodC v s) s)
     (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v s) (prodC v s)
        (identity v) (identity s) · lens_put f)
     (identity s) · BinProductPr1 C (prodC s s)) =
lens_put f

   · (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v s) (prodC v s)
        (identity v) (identity s) · lens_put f)) =

      apply id_left.

C: category
prodC: BinProducts C
s, v: C
f: lens s v
BinProductArrow C (prodC (prodC v s) s)
  (identity (prodC v s)) (BinProductPr2 C (prodC v s))
· (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v s)
     (prodC (prodC v s) s)
     (BinProductOfArrows C (prodC v v) (prodC v s)
        (identity v) (lens_get f)
      · BinProductPr1 C (prodC v v)) (identity s)
   · lens_put f) = lens_put f
